msg:Next city, Manxin Hotel Club, this advertisement is still very attractive. When I came to visit the Great Water Wall, I stayed a day in advance and chose this hotel. As expected, my family was not disappointed.
The hotel is built according to the mountain people. During the day, you can see the pear blossoms on the mountain through the window, which makes you feel good.
The whole facility is great. With Xiaodu's blessing, the whole house is instantly full of smart experiences. If you bring your children here, they will definitely love it.
There is a naughty castle entertainment area on the basement floor of the hotel. Although it is not big, the advantage is that there are almost no people playing there, and it feels really good to reserve the area.
There are charging piles underground in the hotel, and you can also recharge by taking a tram. The most important thing is that the distance between the hotel and the Great Water Wall is only 1.2km, and it only takes 5 minutes to drive, which is really convenient. If you want to avoid traffic jams during holidays, you must leave early!

msg:I have booked hotels on Ctrip so many times, but I have never had such a bad experience as this time. The room type is seriously inconsistent with the house I checked in. The tatami in the photo is only by the window. There is at least a proper bed on the upper floor of the whole house! The upper and lower floors assigned to me are all tatami beds, which is very inconvenient for the elderly to bend their knees! At least put a proper bed for me! Then there is only a TV on the second floor, which is not important. People on the first floor donâ€™t watch it. But all the master control switches and phones are on the second floor. There is no power, phone, or switch at the head of the bed on the first floor. If you turn off the lights upstairs, they will turn them off downstairs together. So it is really inconvenient to go to the front desk to find customer service. The customer service told me that the first floor of this room was not occupied before. Because there were no rooms on May Day, they could not change it for me. I wondered why the photos were completely inconsistent? The price is also set according to the photos! I spent the price of a five-star high-end room and felt that it would be better to sleep in the farmyard next to it for my convenience. It was really an experience I had never had before!
